「ええ。生産量がごく少ないのです。　けれど重量比強度に優れるユーツ鋼は――競技用劔冑の材料としてまさに理想的」
"Yes. The production volume is very low. However, Utsu steel, which has excellent weight-to-weight ratio strength, is ideal as a material for competition helmets."

「これまではごく一部のハイエンドモデルが翼などの重要箇所にだけ用いておりました。　……その最高級鋼材を、よもや、ここまで惜しみなく投入して劔冑を造るとは……」
"Until now, only a small number of high-end models used it only for important parts such as wings .... It is said that the finest steel materials are used so generously to make a helmet ..."

「どうなるんだ？」
"What will happen?"

「え――」
"e--"

異様な光景がそこにあった。　黄金翼の騎士が、ストレートを駆けている。
There was a strange sight there. A golden-winged knight is running straight.

その速さは付近を走る数騎とほぼ同等。　あるいはやや劣るか。　だが、おおむね変わらない程度の速度で――
Its speed is almost the same as several horses running in the vicinity. Or is it slightly inferior? However, at a speed that is almost unchanged--

騎航んでいる。　一周目、スタート直後の騎体が。
I'm riding. On the first lap, the horse body immediately after the start.

「怪物がいる、という事だ。　無論、慣らし運転を充分にこなしていたのだろうが……それにしても」

「異常、という他はない加速性でございます。　完全ユーツ鋼製という特徴がもたらす常識外の軽量さであれを実現しているのでありましょうが……」
"It's an abnormal acceleration. I wonder if it's possible to achieve the unconventional lightness brought about by the characteristic of being made entirely of Utsu steel ..."

「あの加速性は決勝レースで真価を発揮するはず。スタート直後の乱戦をあの威力で切り抜けて、後はひたすらトップを騎航り続けるのでしょう……ね」
"That acceleration should show its true value in the final race. It will survive the turbulent battle immediately after the start with that power, and after that it will continue to ride on the top ..."

それぞれに、呆れる以外にないという表情で感想を呟く俺ほか三名。　いや、俺達だけではなかった。観客らも熱狂を忘れ、ただただ唖然として、疾駆する金色を見つめている。
Each of them, I and three others muttered their impressions with the expression that they had no choice but to be amazed. No, we weren't the only ones. The spectators have forgotten their enthusiasm and are just stunned, staring at the rushing gold.

魅入られたように。　サーキット場としておよそ考えられない静寂の中を、翔京の〝理想〟――ウルティマ・シュールは王者そのものの傲岸ぶりで駆け続ける。
As fascinated. In the silence that is almost unthinkable as a circuit place, Shokyo's "ideal" -Ultima Sur continues to run for the first time in the king's own shore.

二周、三周……　周回を経るにつれ、いよいよその異様な本性は露わになる。
Two laps, three laps ... As the laps go by, the strange nature is finally revealed.

五周目ラップ、一分二六秒八九。　六周目ラップ、一分二六秒四四。　七周目ラップ――
Fifth lap lap, 1 minute 26 seconds 89. Sixth lap lap, 1 minute 26 seconds 44. Seventh lap lap--

周回時間で一秒差。　アーマーレースという競技、この鎌倉サーキットという舞台においては、圧倒的と言っても良い程の差だ。
One second difference in lap time. In the competition of armor race and the stage of this Kamakura circuit, it is an overwhelming difference.

If you look at it, Yokotan Works, who once retired, pulls out the horse body again and appears on the course. ...... It would be useless. Moreover, it is meaningless. Whether you win or lose Ultima in qualifying, the game is not decided.

明日の上位を確保している以上、後は敵の観察だけしておけばいいのだ。　が、そう思いつつも――俺はヨコタンの心情を理解できるような気がしていた。
As long as we have secured the top position tomorrow, all we have to do is observe the enemy. However, while thinking so-I felt like I could understand Yokotan's feelings.

混乱しているのだ。　おそらくは、まともな判断ができなくなるほど。
I'm confused. Perhaps it's hard to make a decent decision.

Even though he was a compatriot of the gambling promotion group, he probably didn't know about this horse. Maybe he was willing to take the lead after gambling, taking the victory in a hurry.

And it has not yet been acknowledged that such a dream was ephemeral.

The strength of the Ultima knight was that it led the viewer to a frenzy, and at the same time, it made me aware of the actual situation of the race that Ichijo had faced, and made me feel confused somewhere in my heart.

I feel that way too. I think it's amazing, but it's hard to praise it honestly.

According to the old chamberlain, a worker carrying the familiar Tamura logo was rushing around the start. There is also a figure that seems to be Mr. Emperor. I'm wearing a hat deeply.

The announcement echoed. The audience buzzed when they knew the appearance of the last big game-somehow, with a sense of in-law.

It can't be helped. Everyone feels that the game has already been seen. The appearance of the nemesis who has fought with Shokyo for many years is not enough to get excited. Such a kind of boring air had been formed.

Looking at the calm state of the staff, it seemed that Samurai Nagakura's words were more convincing. If so, the judgment is correct. There will be nothing to gain from riding with such a monster.

自分より速い走者と共に走ると記録が伸びることが多い、とは云うが。　限度というものがある。兎と亀が競走すれば、普通の亀は途中で馬鹿馬鹿しさに支配されるに違いない。
It's said that running with a runner faster than you often increases your record. There is a limit. If a rabbit and a turtle race, a normal turtle must be dominated by stupidity along the way.

瞬間、それまでとは違う、本物の歓声が上がる。　皇路操はいわゆるカリスマを備えたレーサーだった。普段の静かな物腰、相反して苛烈な騎航、その両者がカクテルされて独特の魅力を形作っている。
At the moment, a real cheer that is different from before rises. Emperor was a racer with so-called charisma. The usual quiet demeanor and the contradictory fierce voyage, both of which are cocktailed to form a unique charm.

彼女の姿にかつての英雄の面影を想う者も多い。　世代の違いを問わず、二代目の皇路は絶大な人気を誇っていた。
Many people think of her appearance as a former hero. Regardless of generation, the second generation Imperial Road was extremely popular.

……しかしそのカリスマへ捧げられるべき声援も、今日ばかりは本人の登場を待たずして色褪せてゆく。　一瞬の沸騰は一瞬で終わり、観客はすぐに、自分らのヒロインが勝利から遥か遠いことを思い出していた。

まばらになってゆくさざめきと拍手を浴びながら、雲間から差す薄い日差しのように彼女は現れる。　父が創り出した劔冑を纏って。
She appears like the faint sunshine shining through the clouds, with sparsely rustling and applause. Wearing the helmet that my father created.

In the circuit. Every light was fixed and every wind stopped the flow.

あらゆる思考が、同じ方向を指した。　停止した世界で、誰もが音のない声で、ただ一言を主張していた。
Every thought pointed in the same direction. In a stopped world, everyone was insisting on a single word with a silent voice.

それは嘗て、どのような企業も、どのようなチームも、造り上げた例のないカタチをしていた。　全く前例の無い、競技用劔冑。
It was once in an unprecedented form for any company, any team. A completely unprecedented competition helmet.

Kabuto? Is this a helmet?

Malformation. Distorted figure. If you stare at it, you may lose your sense of balance.

狂っている。　この造形は、狂っている。
I'm crazy. This modeling is crazy.

この形を造り上げた人間は心を病んでいる。　間違いなく、脳神経系の大切な螺子を一本、外してしまっている。
The person who created this shape is sick. Without a doubt, I have removed one important screw from the cranial nerve system.

頬を掻き毟りたい、そんな狂躁さえ呼び起こされる。　そして、それと糸一筋で危うく均衡を取っているかのような、感慨――
Even such a maniac who wants to scratch his cheeks is evoked. And I feel as if I'm almost in balance with it.

美しい。　いたたまれぬほどに、美しい。
it's beautiful. It's so beautiful that it won't be crushed.

円周率を無理矢理解き明かして形容したかのような流線型のフォルム。　そこにメタリックブルーのカラーリングが重なれば、それは無限の海であり果てなき空だ。
A streamlined form that seems to have been described by forcibly understanding the circumference ratio. If the metallic blue coloring overlaps there, it is an infinite sea and an endless sky.

異界の美。　あってはならないもの。　禁忌の芸巧。
The beauty of another world. Things that shouldn't be there. Contraindicated art.

Horse body name

そうでなくては、あの美しさは有り得ない。　あれは例えば、風雨に削られた岩山が数千年かけて達成する無想の美とは全く違う。　その対極だ。
Otherwise, that beauty is impossible. That is completely different from the unimaginable beauty that a rocky mountain carved by the wind and rain achieves over thousands of years, for example. At the other end of the spectrum.

己の力を過信し盲信した彫刻家が変哲もない石塊を削り、削り続け、原形を失うまでに変貌を遂げさせ、遂に妄想を実現して輝く宝石に造り変えてしまったとでもいうような――横暴極まる美術。
It can be said that a sculptor who overconfided in his own power and blindly believed in it, scraped an ordinary stone block, continued to scrape it, transformed it until it lost its original shape, and finally realized a delusion and turned it into a shining gem. --A domineering art.

そういったものだ。　そこには確かな思想が――妄想がある。
That's it. There is a certain idea-there is a delusion.
